The Password protected option allows you to set an arbitrary password for each post. The Private option hides the post from everyone except editors and administrators. 3553 | Sielç ce espuartâ | Choose what to export
3554 | Tu puedis espuartâ un file dal contignût dal to sît par impuartâlu intune altre instalazion o plateforme. Il file espuartât al sarà un file XML, clamât WXR. 3609 | Cuale ise la diference fra categoriis e tags? Par solit i tags a son peraulis clâf che a identifichin informazions impuartantis tal to post (nons, sogjets, ec.) che a puedin, o ancje no, jessi presints  in altris post, invezit lis categoriis a son sezions predeterminadis. Se tu pensis al to sît tant che un libri, lis categoriis a son il somari e i tags a son i tiermins dal indiç. | What&#8217;s the difference between categories and tags? Normally, tags are ad-hoc keywords that identify important information in your post (names, subjects, etc) that may or may not recur in other posts, while categories are pre-determined sections. If you think of your site like a book, the categories are like the Table of Contents and the tags are like the terms in the index.

=============

Cheste email di debug e ven mandade cuant che tu dopris une version di disvilup di WordPress.

Se tu pensis che chescj erôrs a sedin dovûts a un bug di WordPress, puedistu fâ rapuart?
 * Vierç une discussion tai forum di supuart: https://wordpress.org/support/forum/alphabeta
 * O, se ti va miôr, scrîf un rapuart sul bug: https://core.trac.wordpress.org/

Graciis! -- La scuadre di WordPress | BETA TESTING?
=============

This debugging email is sent when you are using a development version of WordPress.

If you think these failures might be due to a bug in WordPress, could you report it?
 * Open a thread in the support forums: https://wordpress.org/support/forum/alphabeta
 * Or, if you&#8217;re comfortable writing a bug report: https://core.trac.wordpress.org/

Thanks! &#8212; The WordPress Team

5378 | I Super Aministradôrs no puedin plui jessi zontâts inte schermade des Impostazions. Chest ti puarte te pagjine Modifiche Utent dulà che tu puedis selezionâ une casele par garantî i privileçs di Super Aministradôr. | Super admins can no longer be added on the Options screen. You must now go to the list of existing users on Network Admin > Users and click on Username or the Edit action link below that name. This goes to an Edit User page where you can check a box to grant super admin privileges.
